<div class="">
<h2>
<div class="field field--name-field-related-title field--type-string field--label-hidden field__item">Binding corporate rules</div>
</h2>
<div class="part-wrapper regular">
<div class="part1">
<p>CGI is in a unique and strong position to help clients improve their privacy posture. Our expertise in the management of complex projects and technologies contributes to the data privacy compliance priorities of our clients, and enables us to provide innovative services to support clients' compliance priorities.</p>
<p><a aria-label="C.G.I. Binding Corporate Rules" class="btn" href="/en/privacy/binding-corporate-rules">Explore our Binding Corporate Rules</a></p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<section aria-label="Article before main content" class="pre-content" id="precontent-section">
<div class="wrapper-precontent layout-3-items" id="precontent">
<div class="cog--mq">
<article aria-labelledby="precontent-title-1" class="precontent-item">
<a aria-label="Cookie policy" href="/en/privacy/cookie-policy">
<span class="image-wrapper">
<img alt="smiling group of people reading document" src="/sites/default/files/styles/crop_precontent_3_items_layout/public/medium_banner-recruiting-event-01.png?itok=PO2Sy2wO" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
</span>
<div class="text-wrapper">
<h3 id="precontent-title-1">Cookie policy</h3>
<span class="body">
            
            
                                                                Cookies are identifiers that are transferred to your computers hard drive through your web browser to enable our systems to recognize your browser. We use cookies to collect anonymous data that helps us improve your web experience. 
                      </span>
</div>
</a>
</article>
<article aria-labelledby="precontent-title-2" class="precontent-item">
<a aria-label="Web privacy notice" href="/en/privacy/web-privacy-notice">
<span class="image-wrapper">
<img alt="two people sit on sofa having discussion with a laptop" src="/sites/default/files/styles/crop_precontent_3_items_layout/public/two_people_sit_on_a_sofa_having_a_discussion_with_a_laptop_medium.jpg?itok=BW1oE8AS" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
</span>
<div class="text-wrapper">
<h3 id="precontent-title-2">Web privacy notice</h3>
<span class="body">
            
            
                                                                We are transparent about how we use your personal data when visiting our website. The purpose of this website privacy notice is to inform you about our practices in connection with the collection, use and disclosure of personal data. 
                      </span>
</div>
</a>
</article>
<article aria-labelledby="precontent-title-3" class="precontent-item">
<a aria-label="Privacy policy" href="/en/privacy/privacy-policy">
<span class="image-wrapper">
<img alt="person sitting with laptop in office" src="/sites/default/files/styles/crop_precontent_3_items_layout/public/medium-data-privacy-uk.png?itok=-zhO-pRr" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
</span>
<div class="text-wrapper">
<h3 id="precontent-title-3">Privacy policy</h3>
<span class="body">
            
            
                                                                We are committed to maintaining levels of protection of Personal Data aligned to best practices in the industry which, as a minimum, comply with the requirements of the Applicable Data Protection Legislation and CGIs contractual obligations. 
                      </span>
</div>
</a>
</article>
</div>
</div>
</section>

<div class="related-item-wrapper image-wrapper">
<img alt="Consultants monitoring online activities - Responsible business" src="/sites/default/files/styles/crop_precontent_2_items_layout/public/consultants-monitoring-activities-medium.jpg?itok=rgvJoZJl" typeof="foaf:Image"/>
</div>
<div class="related-item-wrapper text-wrapper">
<h3>Responsible business</h3>
<div class="body">
                                      
                          CGI's values form the foundation of our corporate governance practices.  We are proud to operate as a responsible business to balance the interests of our key stakeholders, our clients, our shareholders and our members. 
                      </div>
<a aria-label="Learn more about Responsible business" class="explore-link" href="/en/corporate-social-responsibility/responsible-business">
            Learn more
          </a>
</div>
